    <script>
     timer = 10000
    $(document).ready(function() {
                    // change_card_interval = setInterval(changeCard, timer)
            })

    function changeCard() {
        if (change_card_interval) {
            clearInterval(change_card_interval);
        }
        $('.homepage-card-wrapper').toggleClass('is-flipped')
        change_card_interval = setInterval(changeCard, timer)
    }

    function changeThreeCard() {
        if (change_card_interval) {
            clearInterval(change_card_interval);
        }

        if (flip == 1) {
            timer = 10000
            $('.homepage-card-wrapper').toggleClass('is-flipped')
            setTimeout(function() {
                $('.homepage-card-wrapper > div:nth-child(1)').addClass('homepage-card-back display-none')
            }, 601)
        } else if (flip == 2) {
            timer = 4000
            $('.homepage-card-wrapper').toggleClass('is-flipped')
            $('.homepage-card-wrapper > div:nth-child(3)').removeClass('homepage-card-back display-none')
            setTimeout(function() {
                $('.homepage-card-wrapper > div:nth-child(2)').addClass('display-none')
            }, 601)
        } else if (flip == 3) {
            timer = 10000
            $('.homepage-card-wrapper').toggleClass('is-flipped')
            $('.homepage-card-wrapper > div:nth-child(1)').removeClass('display-none')
            $('.homepage-card-wrapper > div:nth-child(3)').addClass('homepage-card-back display-none')
        } else if (flip == 4) {
            timer = 10000
            $('.homepage-card-wrapper').toggleClass('is-flipped')
            $('.homepage-card-wrapper > div:nth-child(2)').removeClass('homepage-card-back display-none')
            setTimeout(function() {
                $('.homepage-card-wrapper > div:nth-child(1)').addClass('display-none')
            }, 601)
        } else if (flip == 5) {
            timer = 4000
            $('.homepage-card-wrapper').toggleClass('is-flipped')
            $('.homepage-card-wrapper > div:nth-child(3)').removeClass('display-none')
            setTimeout(function() {
                $('.homepage-card-wrapper > div:nth-child(2)').addClass('homepage-card-back')
            }, 601)
        } else if (flip == 6) {
            timer = 10000
            $('.homepage-card-wrapper').toggleClass('is-flipped')
            $('.homepage-card-wrapper > div:nth-child(1)').removeClass('homepage-card-back display-none')
            setTimeout(function() {
                $('.homepage-card-wrapper > div:nth-child(3)').addClass('display-none')
            }, 601)
            flip = 0
        }
        flip += 1
        change_card_interval = setInterval(changeThreeCard, timer)
    }
    </script>

                        .setChannelName('RepublicTV')

                        var that = this;
                        (function(){
                            setTimeout(function(){
                            that.seekingTime=that.currentTime();
                            }, 500);
                        }).call(that);
                    });
                    barc_player.on('play', function() {
                        barc.play();
                    });
                    barc_player.on('pause', function() {
                        barc.pause();
                    });
                    barc_player.on('seeking', function() {
                        barc.seekStart(this.seekingTime);
                    });
                    barc_player.on('seeked', function() {
                        barc.seekEnd(barc_player.currentTime());
                    });
                    barc_player.on('ended', function () {
                        barc.end();
                    });

                        adInfoContext

                            .setIsTrueView(true);

                    });
                    barc_player.on('ads-pause',function() {
                        barc.adPause();
                    });
                    barc_player.on('ads-ad-ended', function() {
                        try { barc.adEnd(); } catch (error) { console.log(error); }

                    });
                    barc_player.on('ads-ad-skipped', function() {
                        barc.adSkip();
                    });
                });
            }
        }
